# <a name="changelog-for-microsoft-graph"></a><span data-ttu-id="9368f-101">Журнал изменений Microsoft Graph</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9368f-101">Changelog for Microsoft Graph</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9368f-102">Этот журнал содержит сведения об изменениях Microsoft Graph, в том числе API Microsoft Graph для конечных точек версии 1.0 и бета-версии.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9368f-102">This changelog covers what's changed in Microsoft Graph, including the v1.0 and beta endpoint Microsoft Graph APIs.</span></span>  

<span data-ttu-id="9368f-103">Дополнительные сведения об известных проблемах с API Microsoft Graph см. в статье [Известные проблемы](known_issues.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9368f-103">For details about known issues with Microsoft Graph APIs, see [Known issues](known_issues.md).</span></span>

### <a name="onedrive"></a><span data-ttu-id="9368f-332">OneDrive</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9368f-332">OneDrive</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="9368f-1452">Дополнение</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9368f-1452">Addition</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="9368f-1453">Бета</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9368f-1453">beta</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="9368f-1454">Добавлены типы ресурсов **booleanColumn**, **calculatedColumn**, **choiceColumn**, **dateTimeColumn**, **lookupColumn**, **numberColumn**, **personOrGroupColumn** и **textColumn**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9368f-1454">Added the **booleanColumn**, **calculatedColumn**, **choiceColumn**, **dateTimeColumn**, **lookupColumn**, **numberColumn**, **personOrGroupColumn**, and **textColumn** resource types.</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="9368f-1455">В объект **site** добавлено свойство **displayName**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9368f-1455">Added the **displayName** property to **site**.</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="9368f-1456">В объект **site** добавлено свойство навигации **columns**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9368f-1456">Added the **columns** navigation property to **site**.</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="9368f-1457">В объект **sharedDriveItem** добавлены свойства навигации **list** и **listItem**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9368f-1457">Added the **list** and **listItem** navigation properties to **sharedDriveItem**.</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="9368f-1458">В объекты **list**, **listItem** и **site** добавлено свойство **sharepointIds**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9368f-1458">Added the **sharepointIds** property to **list** and **listItem**, and **site**.</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="9368f-1459">Добавлен тип ресурса **columnDefinition**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9368f-1459">Added the **columnDefinition** resource type.</span></span>

This means that you will no longer be able to add an invited user to a group using this API. Instead, use the [add member API](https://developer.microsoft.com/en-us/graph/docs/api-reference/v1.0/api/group_post_members) to add a user to a group.</span></span>|

Эти API позволяют безопасно публиковать локальные приложения для пользователей, находящихся за пределами корпоративной сети, используя Azure AD в качестве общей системы управления доступом. These APIs allow for secure publishing of on-premises applications to users outside the corporate network using Azure AD as the common control plane for access. You can use the published APIs to write applications that can retrieve and update various aspects of application proxy, such as _connectors_, _connectorGroups_ and the _onPremisesPublishing_ settings of an application.</span></span>|

### <a name="privileged-identity-management"></a><span data-ttu-id="9368f-2688">Управление привилегированными пользователями (PIM)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9368f-2688">Privileged Identity Management</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="9368f-2689">**Тип изменения**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9368f-2689">**Change type**</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9368f-2690">**Версия**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9368f-2690">**Version**</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9368f-2691">**Описание**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9368f-2691">**Description**</span></span>|
|:--------------|:-----------|:--------------|
|<span data-ttu-id="9368f-2692">Дополнение</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9368f-2692">Addition</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9368f-2693">Бета</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9368f-2693">Beta</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9368f-p159">Теперь REST API управления привилегированными пользователями доступны в конечной точке Microsoft Graph (бета-версия). [Управление привилегированными пользователями](https://azure.microsoft.com/en-us/documentation/articles/active-directory-privileged-identity-management-configure/) обеспечивает активацию "точно в срок" для привилегированных ролей в организации Azure AD, например ролей глобального администратора, администратора выставления счетов и т. д. C помощью опубликованных API разработчики могут создавать приложения, которые получают и обновляют привилегированные роли и активируют роли для пользователей. Дополнительные сведения см. в статьях [Microsoft Graph: доступна бета-версия API для Azure AD Privileged Identity Management](http://dev.office.com/blogs/microsoft-graph-azure-ad-privileged-identity-management-apis-beta) и [Azure AD Privileged Identity Management](https://developer.microsoft.com/en-us/graph/docs/api-reference/beta/resources/privilegedidentitymanagement_root).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9368f-p159">Privileged Identity Management (PIM) REST APIs now are available in the Microsoft Graph beta endpoint. [Privileged Identity Management](https://azure.microsoft.com/en-us/documentation/articles/active-directory-privileged-identity-management-configure/) provides just in time activation for privileged Azure AD organizational roles such as Global Administrator, Billing Administrator, and so on. You can use the published APIs to write applications that retrieve and update privileged role assignments, and activate users into roles. For details, see [Microsoft Graph: Azure AD Privileged Identity Management Preview APIs available in Beta](http://dev.office.com/blogs/microsoft-graph-azure-ad-privileged-identity-management-apis-beta) and [Azure AD Privileged Identity Management](https://developer.microsoft.com/en-us/graph/docs/api-reference/beta/resources/privilegedidentitymanagement_root).</span></span>|

### <a name="administrative-units"></a><span data-ttu-id="9368f-2699">Административные единицы</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9368f-2699">Administrative Units</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="9368f-2700">**Тип изменения**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9368f-2700">**Change type**</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9368f-2701">**Версия**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9368f-2701">**Version**</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9368f-2702">**Описание**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9368f-2702">**Description**</span></span>|
|:--------------|:-----------|:--------------|
|<span data-ttu-id="9368f-2703">Дополнение</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9368f-2703">Addition</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9368f-2704">Бета</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9368f-2704">Beta</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9368f-p160">Представлен новый API Administrative Units (предварительная версия). Подразделения могут представлять регионы, отделы, места возникновения затрат и т. д. Теперь ими можно управлять с помощью API Microsoft Graph.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9368f-p160">Introduced the new Administrative Unites preview API. Administrative units allow organizations to subdivide their Azure Active Directory, and delegate administrative duties to those subdivisions. Subdivisions can represent regions, departments, cost centers, etc. This can now be managed through the Microsoft Graph API.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="9368f-2817">Дополнение</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9368f-2817">Addition</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9368f-2818">Бета</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9368f-2818">Beta</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9368f-p167">Теперь Azure Active Directory используется в качестве резервного ресурса для запросов /beta/users/id/photo, когда приложению Outlook не удается обслужить запрос (например, когда у пользователя нет лицензии на почтовый ящик или у клиента нет подписки на Exchange Online). ПРИМЕЧАНИЕ. Example: GET https://graph.microsoft.com/v1.0/users?$filter=id+eq+'x'</span></span><br/><span data-ttu-id="9368f-p176">Ранее в запросах POST требовалось добавлять microsoft.graph перед именем функции или действия. Например: POST https://graph.microsoft.com/v1.0/me/Microsoft.Graph.getMemberGroups.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9368f-p176">Previously, any POST requests to service actions and functions require prefixing the action or function name with the microsoft.graph prefix. For example: POST https://graph.microsoft.com/v1.0/me/Microsoft.Graph.getMemberGroups.</span></span><br/><span data-ttu-id="9368f-p177">Теперь не требуется указывать префикс (хотя его по-прежнему можно указывать). Таким образом, указанный ниже запрос также будет работать. POST https://graph.microsoft.com/v1.0/me/getMemberGroups</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9368f-p177">The prefix is now no longer required (although it can still be specified). So the following would now also work: POST https://graph.microsoft.com/v1.0/me/getMemberGroups.</span></span>|

Изначально для управления поведением групп Office использовался только этот шаблон.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9368f-p178">We've added the capability to discover (through _directorySettingTemplates_) and override the default behavior (by creating a _setting_ from the template) for entities and their associated functionality.
